DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim AS build
  # Set architecture and environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=UTC \
      ARCH=x86_64
  # Install base dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      clang \
      llvm \
      libfuzzer-dev \
      afl++ \
      valgrind \
      kcov \
      linux-perf \
      git \
      wget \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install additional optimization tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      libomp-dev \
      libatomic1 \
      libgtest-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Create workspace and copy repository
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  # Configure and build
  RUN mkdir -p build && \
      cd build && \
      cmake -G Ninja \
            -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
            -DARCHITECTURE=${ARCH} \
            -DENABLE_OPTIMIZATIONS=ON \
            .. && \
      ninja
  # Runtime container
  FROM debian:12-slim
  # Copy built artifacts from build stage
  COPY --from=build /workspace /workspace
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      libatomic1 \
      libomp5 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory and entrypoint
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

      cd build && \

            -DSIMDJSON_SANITIZE=OFF \

      ninja && \
      ninja install
